### Probability Mass Function

![Graph with seats probability mass function not yet produced](average-seats-pmf-coaliciócompromísgreensefa.png "Seats Probability Mass Function")

The following table shows the probability mass function per seat for the [poll average](average.html) for Coalició Compromís (Greens/EFA).

| Number of Seats | Probability | Accumulated | Special Marks |
|:---------------:|:-----------:|:-----------:|:-------------:|
| 0 | 5% | 100% | Last Result |
| 1 | 74% | 95% | Median |
| 2 | 20% | 21% |  |
| 3 | 0.4% | 0.4% |  |
| 4 | 0% | 0% |  |
